add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Annexation Start
	id = annex.event
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.event" }
	title = annex.event.t
	desc = annex.event.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = annex.event.a
		country_event = {
			id = annex.9999
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.event.b
		set_global_flag = START_ANNEXATION_EVENTS
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}
country_event = { #Annexation Start
	id = annex.9999
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.9999" }
	title = annex.9999.t
	desc = annex.9999.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = annex.9999.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = annex_9999_tt
	}	
	option = {
		name = annex.9999.b
		set_global_flag = START_ANNEXATION_EVENTS
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Check for possible annexations
	id = annex.1
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			# Special tags - these shouldn't exist outside of very specific circumstances
			tag = ATU #debug tag
			AND = {
				has_civil_war = yes
				any_enemy_country = {
					is_dynamic_country = yes
					civilwar_target = ROOT #== start_civil_war
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { global.annexation_relevant_states = THIS }
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					has_state_flag = occupied_by_@ROOT
				}
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
			check_potential_annexations = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = RF_checking_for_possible_annexations
	}
}

country_event = { #Switzerland liberation
	id = annex.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.2" }
	title = annexation_SWI_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SWI_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = FRA
				AND = {
					tag = GER
					has_completed_focus = GER_pangermanic_rhetoric
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			ITA = { transfer_state = 845 add_state_core = 845 }
			SWI = { set_country_flag = ITA_nittified }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SWI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SWI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			SWI = { set_cosmetic_tag = SWI_socialist_puppet }
			country_event = germany.46
		}
	}

	option = { #Partition Switzerland
		name = annex.2.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point } }
			OR = {
				17 = { is_core_of = var:17.owner var:17.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				50 = { is_core_of = var:50.owner var:50.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				159 = { is_core_of = var:159.owner var:159.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = FRA }
			FRA = { add_state_core = 846 }
			FIU = { add_state_core = 845 }
			BAV = {
				add_state_core = 3
				add_state_core = 151
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = FIU
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				FIU = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BAV
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				BAV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { BAV = { has_cosmetic_tag = BAV_FRA_escadron } } }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BAV }
				puppet_released_tag = yes
				BAV = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = BAV_FRA_escadron
					set_politics = { ruling_party = despotism }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = despotism
						popularity = 0.30
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { var:17.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				846 = { add_core_of = var:17.owner }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = var:17.owner
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
					var:17.owner = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:50.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				3 = { add_core_of = var:50.owner }
				151 = { add_core_of = var:50.owner }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = var:50.owner
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
					var:50.owner = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:159.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				159 = { add_core_of = var:159.owner }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = var:159.owner
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
					var:159.owner = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SWI_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #French liberation
	id = annex.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.3" }
	title = annexation_FRA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_FRA_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = FRA }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 19 #Aquitaine
						state = 31 #Midi Pyrenees
						state = 22 #Languedoc
						state = 20 #Rhone
						state = 26 #Auvergne
						state = 25 #Limousin
						state = 23 #Poitou
						state = 33 #Centre-Sud
						state = 24 #Centre
						state = 30 #Loire
						state = 15 #Normandy
						state = 785 #Picardy
						state = 16 #Ile De France
						state = 27 #Bourgogne
						state = 18 #Champange
						state = 920 #Upper lorraine
						state = 17 #Franche-Comte
						state = 735 #Savoy
						state = 32 #Alpes
						state = 21 #Provence
						state = 1 #Corsica
						state = 1264 #Nice
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FRA
			}
			set_province_name = { id = 11506 name = GER_decision_GER_france_release_province_11506 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = fra_acephale
							has_country_flag = fra_escadron
						}
					}
				}
				FRA = { clr_country_flag = PREV }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate Entire France
		name = annex.3.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		if = {			##### GERMAN RELEASE #####
			limit = { tag = GER }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 14 #Brittany
						state = 32 #Alpes
						state = 21 #Provence
						state = 735 #Savoy
						state = 1 #Corsica
						state = 1264 #Nice
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FRA
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GER_prison_house_thesis }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 34 #Wallonia
							state = 958 #East Wallonia
							state = 29 #Pas de Calais
							state = 938 #Calais
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FRA
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = FRA }
				add_core_of = SFR
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SFR
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				SFR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SFR }
			puppet_released_tag = yes

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_deat_win }
				SFR = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = popular_socialism
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = popular_socialism
						popularity = 0.30
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = SFR_deat
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_pierre_win }
				SFR = {
					set_politics = { ruling_party = revisionist_socialism }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = revisionist_socialism
						popularity = 0.30
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = SFR_pierre
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_pelletier_win }
				SFR = {
					set_politics = { ruling_party = vanguard_socialism }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = vanguard_socialism
						popularity = 0.30
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = SFR_pelletier
				}
			}
		}
		else = {			##### STANDARD RELEASE #####
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 14 #Brittany
						state = 32 #Alpes
						state = 21 #Provence
						state = 735 #Savoy
						state = 1 #Corsica
						state = 1264 #Nice
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FRA
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = FRA
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				FRA = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FRA }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Partition France
		name = annex.3.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = GER }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		if = { ########### ITALIAN RELEASE SCHEIßE ###########
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1
						state = 735
						state = 21
						state = 32
						state = 1264
						state = 1264
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ITA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 29 #Pas de Calais
						state = 938 #Calais
					}
				}
				add_core_of = FRA
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				FRA = { set_country_flag = ITA_nittified add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = medium_increase } }
				ITA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = medium_increase } }
			}
		}

		#################### DEFAULT RELEASE/COSMETIC TAG SCHEIßE ##########
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = FRA
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			FRA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				state = 14 #Brittany
			}
			add_core_of = BRT
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			BRT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FRA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BRT }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = FRA_CONQ
		occupy_large_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #German liberation
	id = annex.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.4" }
	title = annexation_GER_CONQ
	desc = annexation_GER_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = GER }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 64 #Brandenburg
						state = 63 #Hinterpommern
						state = 68 #Ostmark
						state = 66 #Lower Silesia
						state = 62 #Pommern
						state = 61 #Mecklenburg
						state = 65 #Sachsen
						state = 59 #Hannover
						state = 56 #Wesser-Ems
						state = 57 #Westfalen
						state = 55 #Hessen
						state = 60 #Thuringen
						state = 991 #Frankfurt
					}
				}
				add_core_of = GER
			}
			if = { ### BECOME GERMANY TAGS
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PRS
						AND = {
							tag = AUS
							OR = {
								has_completed_focus = AUS_reclaim_urheimat
								has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business
							}
						} 
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 53 #Niederbayern
							state = 52 #Oberbayern
							state = 50 #Wurttemberg
							state = 42 #Moselland
							state = 844 #West Rhineland
							state = 51 #East Rhineland
							state = 54 #Franken
							is_core_of = GER
						}
					}
					add_core_of = GER
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate Entire Germany
		name = annex.4.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = PRS
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = AUS_reclaim_urheimat
						has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business
					}
				} 
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = { PRS = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 53 #Niederbayern
						state = 54 #Franken
						state = 52 #Oberbayern
						state = 50 #Wurttemberg
						state = 42 #Moselland
						state = 844 #West Rhineland
						state = 51 #East Rhineland
						is_core_of = GER
					}
				}
				add_core_of = GER
				add_core_of = PRS
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PRS
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				PRS = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			PRS = { set_cosmetic_tag = PRS_GER }
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				GER = { add_state_core = 8 set_country_flag = ITA_nittified }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 53 #Niederbayern
						state = 54 #Franken
						state = 52 #Oberbayern
						state = 50 #Wurttemberg
						state = 42 #Moselland
						state = 844 #West Rhineland
						state = 51 #East Rhineland
					}
				}
				add_core_of = GER
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = GER
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				GER = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GER }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Decide what to do with each region
		name = annex.4.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = PRS
				tag = FRA
				PRS = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = AUS_reclaim_urheimat
						has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business
					}
				}
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GER
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			GER = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GER }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Take the mantle of Germany
		name = annex.4.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = PRS
				AND = { tag = AUS OR = { has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business has_completed_focus = AUS_reclaim_urheimat } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = PRS }
			set_cosmetic_tag = PRS_GER
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 53 #Niederbayern
						state = 54 #Franken
						state = 52 #Oberbayern
						state = 50 #Wurttemberg
						state = 42 #Moselland
						state = 844 #West Rhineland
						state = 51 #East Rhineland
						is_core_of = GER
					}
				}
				add_core_of = AUS
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_mises_confed
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CZE
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				CZE = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CZE }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			CZE = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_mises_puppet
				promote_character = CZE_Karel_Englis
			}
			SLV = {
				add_state_core = 102
				transfer_state = 102
				AUS = {
					remove_state_core = 102
					add_state_claim = 102
					set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SLV }
					puppet_released_tag = yes
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = SLV_mises_puppet
				set_politics = { ruling_party = progressivism }
				add_popularity = { ideology = progressivism popularity = 0.4 }
				promote_character = SLV_drago
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				AND = { tag = AUS OR = { has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business has_completed_focus = AUS_reclaim_urheimat } }
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_CONQ
		occupy_large_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #U.K. liberation
	id = annex.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.5" }
	title = annexation_ENG_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ENG_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = ENG }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 131 #Northern England
						state = 130 #Yorkshire
						state = 132 #Lancashire
						state = 128 #West Midlands
						state = 129 #East Midlands
						state = 125 #East Anglia
						state = 126 #Greater London Area
						state = 338 #Gloucestershire
						state = 127 #Sussex
						state = 123 #Cornwall
						state = 1187 #West Country
						state = 1184 #Hampshire
						state = 1183 #Essex
						state = 1179 #Marches
						state = 1168 #Northumberland
						state = 1186 #Great Ouse
						state = 1182 #Lincolnshire
						state = 1185 #Thames
						state = 966 #Channel isles						
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ENG
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate United Kingdom
		name = annex.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					#Scotland
					state = 1169 #Scottish Border
					state = 133 #Dumfries & Galloway
					state = 1172 #Lanarkshire
					state = 1171 #Ochils & Fife
					state = 136 #Aberdeenshire
					state = 120 #Scottish Highlands
					state = 1170 #Argyll & Bute
					state = 121 #Lothian
					#Wales
					state = 1180 #Gwynedd
					state = 1181 #Dyfed
					state = 1178 #Powys
					state = 122 #Glamorganshire
				}
			}
			add_core_of = ENG
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ENG
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			base = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				FIU = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		
		if = {		##### GERMAN RELEASE #####
			limit = { tag = GER }
			1200 = { add_core_of = ITA }
			1262 = { remove_core_of = ITA }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ITA
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			puppet_released_tag = yes

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_basso_win }
				ITA = {
					promote_character = ITA_lelio_basso
					set_politics = { 
						ruling_party = popular_socialism
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = popular_socialism
						popularity = 0.23
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ITA_basso
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_ricci_win }
				ITA = {
					promote_character = ITA_berto_ricci
					set_politics = { 
						ruling_party = vanguard_socialism
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = vanguard_socialism
						popularity = 0.23
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ITA_ricci
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_rosselli_win }
				ITA = {
					promote_character = ITA_carlo_rosselli
					set_politics = { 
						ruling_party = progressivism
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = progressivism
						popularity = 0.23
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ITA_republic
				}
			}
		}
		else = {		##### STANDARD RELEASE #####
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ITA
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ITA }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}

		}
	}

country_event = { #Czech Liberation
	id = annex.12
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.12" }
	title = annexation_CZE_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CZE_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = CZE }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 9 #Bohemia
						state = 75 #Morovia
					}
				}
				add_core_of = CZE
			}
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate
		name = annex.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = { ###### UNIQUE RELEASE SCHEIßE #####
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 69
						state = 913
						state = 74
						state = 72
						state = 70
						state = 664
						state = 71
						state = 73
						state = 1148
					}
				}
				CZE = { add_state_core = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CZE
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				CZE = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CZE }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			
			CZE = { set_country_flag = ITA_nittified set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_czechoslovakia }
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = FRA }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 69
							state = 74
							state = 9
							state = 75
							state = 913
						}
					}
					CZE = { add_state_core = PREV }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				CZE = { set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_socialist_puppet }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_bolen_win }
					CZE = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = vanguard_socialism
							elections_allowed = no			
						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = vanguard_socialism
							popularity = 0.20
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_bolen_win
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_stribny_win }
					CZE = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = revisionist_socialism
							elections_allowed = no			
						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = revisionist_socialism
							popularity = 0.20
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_stribny_win
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_verbnsky }
					CZE = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = popular_socialism
							elections_allowed = no			
						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = popular_socialism
							popularity = 0.20
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_verbnsky
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_patejdl }
					CZE = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = progressivism
							elections_allowed = no			
						}
						set_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = progressivism
							popularity = 0.20
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_patejdl
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_hasek }
					CZE = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = anarchism
							elections_allowed = no			
						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = anarchism
							popularity = 0.20
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_hasek
					}
				}
			}

			###### STANDARD RELEASE SCHEIßE #####
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CZE
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				CZE = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CZE }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to Austria
		name = annex.12.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			has_reactionary_government = yes
			AUS = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 913 #South Sudetenland
					is_core_of = CZE
				}
			}
			add_core_of = AUS
			AUS = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CZE
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				AND = { tag = AUS has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business }
				tag = FRA
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = CZE_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Luxembourg Liberation
	id = annex.15
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.15" }
	title = annexation_LUX_CONQ
	desc = annexation_LUX_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				AUS = { is_ally_with = ROOT owns_state = 844 }
			}
			AUS = { save_event_target_as = german_ally }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { is_ally_with = ROOT owns_state = 844 }
			}
			GER = { save_event_target_as = german_ally }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PRS = { is_ally_with = ROOT owns_state = 844 }
			}
			PRS = { save_event_target_as = german_ally }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				RHI = { is_ally_with = ROOT owns_state = 844 }
			}
			RHI = { save_event_target_as = german_ally }
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.15.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LUX
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			LUX = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LUX }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to Germany
		name = annex.15.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			event_target:german_ally = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LUX
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			add_core_of = event_target:german_ally
			event_target:german_ally = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = annex.integrate
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FRA
				tag = GER
				has_country_flag = is_germany
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					has_country_flag = is_germany
				}
			}
			8 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			8 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LUX_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }

		}

		}

				}
			}
			add_core_of = BEL
		}
		every_owned_state = {

				is_core_of = BEL
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			BEL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BEL }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes

		recheck_annexations = yes

			}
		}

			base = 100
		}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.19.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SPR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SPR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SPR }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		if = { ########### UNIQUE RELEASE SCHEIßE ###########
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			hidden_effect = {
				SPR = {
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = medium_increase }
					set_politics = { ruling_party = progressivism }
					add_popularity = { ideology = progressivism popularity = 0.4 }
				}
				ITA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SPR modifier = medium_increase } }
			}
		}

				}

country_event = { #Hungarian Liberation
	id = annex.31
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.31" }
	title = annexation_HUN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_HUN_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = HUN }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 155 #Transdanubia
						state = 43 #Northern Hungary
						state = 154 #Alfold
						state = 1147
					}
				}
				add_core_of = HUN
			}
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = annex.31.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = { ###### UNIQUE RELEASE SCHEIßE #####
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 45
						state = 1035
						state = 923
						state = 911
					}
				}
				HUN = { add_state_core = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = HUN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				HUN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HUN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			HUN = { set_country_flag = ITA_nittified }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 911
						state = 664
						state = 73
						state = 1148
					}
				}
				HUN = { add_state_core = PREV }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { OR = { state = 901 } }
				HUN = { add_state_claim = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = HUN
						is_claimed_by = HUN
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				HUN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HUN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			HUN = {
				set_politics = { ruling_party = right_authoritarianism }
				add_popularity = { ideology = right_authoritarianism popularity = 0.4 }
				set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_mises_puppet
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = HUN_Miklos_Horthy
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = anocracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = { ###### STANDARD RELEASE SCHEIßE #####
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = HUN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				HUN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HUN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				AND = { tag = AUS has_completed_focus = AUS_open_for_business }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}

country_event = { #Norwegian Liberation
	id = annex.36
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.36" }
	title = annexation_NOR_CONQ
	desc = annexation_NOR_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = NOR }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 110 #Ostlandet
						state = 784 #Syndlander
						state = 142 #Vestlandet
						state = 143 #Trondelag
						state = 144 #Nord-Norge
						state = 847 #Finnmark
					}
				}
				add_core_of = NOR
			}
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.36.a
		trigger = { NOT = { NRO = { is_ally_with = ROOT } } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = NOR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			NOR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NOR }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to Norway
		name = annex.36.b
		trigger = {
			country_exists = NRO
			NOT = { OR = { has_socialist_government = yes } }
			OR = {
				NRO = { is_ally_with = ROOT } #Same Faction as Norway
				ENG = { is_ally_with = ROOT } #Is in Entente Faction
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = NOR }
		remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 110 #Ostlandet
					state = 784 #Syndlander
					state = 142 #Vestlandet
					state = 143 #Trondelag
					state = 144 #Nord-Norge
					state = 847 #Finnmark
				}
			}
			add_core_of = NRO
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = NRO
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			NRO = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = NOR_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}
country_event = { #Irish Liberation
	id = annex.37
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.37" }
	title = annexation_IRE_CONQ
	desc = annexation_IRE_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.37.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = { #Liberate Under Northern Ireland
			limit = { tag = ENG }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = IRE
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				NIR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
		else = { #STANDARD RELEASE
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = IRE
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				IRE = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = IRE }
			puppet_released_tag = yes

			if = {
				limit = { tag = GER }
				IRE = {
					promote_character = IRE_paddy_o_daire
					set_politics = { ruling_party = popular_socialism }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = popular_socialism
						popularity = 0.23
					}
				}
				country_event = germany.40
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Direct Rule from London
		name = annex.37.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = ENG
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = IRE
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = NIR
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

	id = annex.40
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.40" }

	desc = annexation_LAT_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.40.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			LAT = {
				set_country_flag = ITA_nittified
				set_politics = { ruling_party = progressivism }
				add_popularity = { ideology = progressivism popularity = 0.4 }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LAT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			LAT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LAT }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LAT_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Novorossyia Liberation

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.44" }
	title = annexation_SRU_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SRU_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = SRU }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.44.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 224 #Starodub
					state = 854 #Chernigov
					state = 225 #Sumy
					state = 259 #Poltava
					state = 221 #Kharkov
					state = 228 #Lugansk
					state = 227 #Yuzovka
					state = 853 #Yekaterinoslav
					state = 200 #Alexandrovsk
					state = 196 #Melitopol
					state = 137 #Crimea
				}
			}
			add_core_of = SRU
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ROS = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						#Non-Ukraine
						state = 222 #Orel
						state = 258 #Livny
						state = 220 #Kursk
						state = 240 #Belgorod
						state = 859 #Ostrogozhsk
						state = 260 #Voronezh
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROS
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROS
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ROS = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						#Non-Ukraine
						state = 222 #Orel
						state = 258 #Livny
						state = 220 #Kursk
						state = 240 #Belgorod
						state = 859 #Ostrogozhsk
						state = 260 #Voronezh
					}
				}
				add_core_of = var:219.owner
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = var:219.owner
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				var:219.owner = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SRU
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRU = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRU }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		
		SRU = { set_cosmetic_tag = SRU_non_rus }
	}
	
	option = { #Give to Ukraine
		name = annex.44.b
		trigger = {
			UKR = { exists = yes }
			AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				UKR = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 224 #Starodub
					state = 854 #Chernigov
					state = 225 #Sumy
					state = 259 #Poltava
					state = 221 #Kharkov
					state = 228 #Lugansk
					state = 227 #Yuzovka
					state = 853 #Yekaterinoslav
					state = 200 #Alexandrovsk
					state = 196 #Melitopol
					state = 137 #Crimea
				}
			}
			add_core_of = UKR
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = UKR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			UKR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ROS = { is_ally_with = ROOT }

				}

			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate United Baltics
		name = annex.45.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 13 #Revel

				}

			add_core_of = WRU
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WRU
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			WRU = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		if = {			#Giving Shite to Russia
			limit = {
				ROS = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 209 #Pskov

					OR = {
						state = 209 #Pskov

						state = 857 #Vitebsk

			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = var:219.owner
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes

country_event = { #Fate of Posen REGION
	id = annex.169
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.169" }
	title = annexation_POSEN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_POSEN_CONQ_desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Give it to Poland
		name = annex.169.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = GER
			}
			POL = {
				is_ally_with = ROOT
				owns_state = 87
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		86 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = POL
						is_core_of = POL
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = POL
			}
			POL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	
	option = { #Give it to the Germans
		name = annex.169.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = GER
			}
			var:66.owner = {
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				POL = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			GER = { save_event_target_as = german_ally }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PRS = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			PRS = { save_event_target_as = german_ally }
		}
		86 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = event_target:german_ally }
				remove_claim_by = event_target:german_ally
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = event_target:german_ally } }
				add_core_of = event_target:german_ally
			}
			event_target:german_ally = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.169.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = POL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		86 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = POSEN_CONQ
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RHI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.integrate
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FRA
				tag = GER
				has_country_flag = is_germany
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
				has_country_flag = is_germany
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 51 #East Rhineland
						state = 844 #West Rhineland
						state = 42 #Rheinpfalz
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 51 #East Rhineland
						state = 844 #West Rhineland
						state = 42 #Rheinpfalz
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = RHI_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes

country_event = { #Lorraine liberation

	title = annexation_LOR_CONQ
	desc = annexation_LOR_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.175.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = FRA
				tag = GER
				tag = PRS
				has_country_flag = is_germany
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 959 #Lothringen
						state = 956 #Lorraine Francaise
						state = 957 #Alsace Francaise
						state = 28 #Elsass
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				add_core_of = LOR
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LOR
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				LOR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LOR }
			puppet_released_tag = yes

			LOR = { set_country_flag = ITA_nittified set_cosmetic_tag = LOR_alsace }
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 959 #Lothringen
						state = 956 #Lorraine Francaise
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				add_core_of = LOR
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LOR
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				LOR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LOR }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to the French
		name = annex.175.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				tag = FRA
				tag = GER
				tag = PRS
				has_country_flag = is_germany
			}
			FRA = {
				is_ally_with = ROOT
				owns_state = 920
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 959
					state = 956
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = FRA }
				remove_claim_by = FRA
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = FRA } }
				add_core_of = FRA
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = ROOT is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
				FRA = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

			}

			}

			}
			if = {

			if = {

			}
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = HUN
				tag = CRO
				tag = SER
				tag = YUG
			}
			HUN = {
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		45 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = HUN }
				remove_claim_by = HUN
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = HUN } }
				add_core_of = HUN
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
				HUN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {

				tag = HUN

				tag = YUG
				tag = SER
			}

			base = 1000
		}

					state = 45 #Vojvodina
				}

country_event = { #North Macedonia liberation
	id = annex.202
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.202" }
	title = annexation_NORMACEDONIA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_NORMACEDONIA_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				YUG = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			YUG = { save_event_target_as = serb_ally }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				SER = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			SER = { save_event_target_as = serb_ally }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Liberate Macedonia
		name = annex.202.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = YUG
				tag = SER
				tag = BUL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 106
					state = 1062
				}
			}
			add_core_of = MAC
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MAC
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			MAC = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MAC }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to Bulgaria
		name = annex.202.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = YUG
				tag = SER
				tag = BUL
			}
			BUL = {
				owns_state = 1064
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				BUL = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { owns_state = 1062 }
			}
			1062 = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = BUL }
					remove_claim_by = BUL
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = BUL } }
					add_core_of = BUL
				}
				if = { limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { owns_state = 106 }
			}
			106 = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = BUL }
					remove_claim_by = BUL
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = BUL } }
					add_core_of = BUL
				}
				if = { limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to Serbia
		name = annex.202.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = YUG
				tag = SER
				tag = BUL
			}
			SER = {
				owns_state = 1063
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				SER = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { owns_state = 106 }
			}
			106 = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SER }
					remove_claim_by = SER
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SER } }
					add_core_of = SER
				}
				if = { limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					SER = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { owns_state = 1062 }
			}
			1062 = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SER }
					remove_claim_by = SER
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SER } }
					add_core_of = SER
				}
				if = { limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					SER = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Porque no los dos
		name = annex.202.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = YUG
				tag = SER
				tag = BUL
			}
			ROOT = {
				owns_state = 106
				owns_state = 1062
			}
			AND = {
				BUL = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					OR = {
						owns_state = 48
						owns_state = 812
					}
				}
				event_target:serb_ally = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					owns_state = 1063
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
		1062 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = BUL }
				remove_claim_by = BUL
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = BUL } }
				add_core_of = BUL
			}
			if = { limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
				BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		106 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = event_target:serb_ally }
				remove_claim_by = event_target:serb_ally
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = event_target:serb_ally } }
				add_core_of = event_target:serb_ally
			}
			if = { limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
				event_target:serb_ally = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.integrate
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = YUG
				tag = SER
				tag = BUL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 106 #North Macedonia
					state = 1062 #Pirin Macedonia
				}
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = NORMACEDONIA_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 39 #Alto Adige
						state = 1200 #Trentino
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SOUTH_TYROL_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Australia Liberation
	id = annex.78
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.78" }
	title = annexation_AST_CONQ
	desc = annexation_AST_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.78.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 801 #Northwestern Australia
					state = 522 #Western Australia
					state = 803 #Southwestern Australia
				}
			}
			add_core_of = AST
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			AST = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AST }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = ENG }
			}
			AST = { set_cosmetic_tag = AST_independent }
		}
	}

	option = { #Split Australia
		name = annex.78.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			AST = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WAS
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			WAS = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AST }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = WAS }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ENG }
			AST = { set_cosmetic_tag = AST_eastralia }
		}
		else = {
			AST = { set_cosmetic_tag = AST_independent }
			WAS = { set_cosmetic_tag = WAS_independent }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = PAL }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate a United Levant
		name = annex.182.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1092 #Golan
					state = 554 #Damascus
					state = 1052 #Deir-az-Zur

					state = 680 #Diyar Mudar
					state = 1085 #

					state = 455 #
					state = 1003 #
					state = 1004 #
					state = 454 #

			}

		}

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SYR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes

		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}
	option = { #Split the Levant in two
		name = annex.182.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 554 #Damascus
					state = 1052 #Deir-az-Zur
					state = 677 #Aleppo
					state = 680 #Diyar Mudar
					state = 1085 #
					state = 1086 #
					state = 553 #
					state = 1091 #
				}
			}

		}

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SYR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SYR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1092 #
					state = 1089 #
					state = 455 #
					state = 1003 #
					state = 1004 #
					state = 454 #
				}
			}
			add_core_of = PAL
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PAL
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			PAL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SYR }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PAL }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}
	option = { #Balkanize the Levant
		name = annex.182.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 1085 #Alexandretta
				owns_state = 1086 #Alawite
				owns_state = 553 #Lebanon
				owns_state = 1091 #Jabal Al-Druze
				owns_state = 455 #Transjordan
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 1085 is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }

				add_core_of = CCD
				transfer_state_to = CCD
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CCD }
			puppet_released_tag = yes

				transfer_state_to = DRZ
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DRZ }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
		if = {

			553 = {
				add_core_of = LEB
				transfer_state_to = LEB
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LEB }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
		if = {

			every_state = {

						state = 455
						state = 1089
					}
				}
				add_core_of = JOR
			}

					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = JOR }

				}
			}
			add_core_of = SYR
		}

				is_core_of = SYR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SYR = { transfer_state = PREV }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.111.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = { #### UNIQUE RELEASE ####
			limit = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BRA
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							state = 300
							state = 301
							state = 688
							state = 302
							state = 487
						}
					}
				}
				BRR = { add_state_core = PREV }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BRR
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				BRR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			BRR = {
				set_politics = { ruling_party = liberalism }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = liberalism
					popularity = 0.4
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = progressivism
					popularity = 0.1
				}
			}
		}
		else = { #### STANDARD RELEASE ####
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BRA
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				BRA = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BRA }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = BRA_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Algerian Liberation
	id = annex.121
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.121" }
	title = annexation_ALG_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ALG_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = ALG }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 459 #Algiers
						state = 460 #Constantine
						state = 513 #Tlemcen
						state = 1006 #Adrar
						state = 514 #Algerian Desert
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ALG
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.121.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALG
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ALG = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALG }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			ALG = {
				set_politics = { 
					ruling_party = vanguard_socialism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = vanguard_socialism
					popularity = 0.30
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate North African Federation
		name = annex.121.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
				tag = GER
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 514
					state = 1006
					state = 513
					state = 459
					state = 460
					state = 458
					state = 665
					state = 661 #Tripolitania
					state = 448 #Tripoli
					state = 449 #El Agheila
					state = 662 #Sirte
					state = 450 #Benghasi
					state = 663 #Cyrenaica
					state = 451 #Derna
					state = 273 #Libyan Desert
					state = 1199 #Fezzan
					state = 699
					state = 462
					state = 783
					state = 969
					state = 971
					state = 1006
					state = 972
					state = 290
					state = 970
					state = 767
					state = 551
					state = 552
					state = 456
					state = 457
					state = 452
					state = 447
					state = 446
					state = 800
					state = 453
					state = 461
					state = 1119
					state = 1120
					state = 1121
					state = 968
					state = 967
				}
			}
			ALG = { add_state_core = PREV }
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALG
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ALG = { transfer_state = PREV}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALG }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		
		ALG = { set_cosmetic_tag = ALG_AMU }
	}

	option = { #Give to French Ally
		name = annex.give_fra
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				FRA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }		
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point } }
			has_socialist_government = no
			FRA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALG
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			FRA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { ##### LIBERAL ITALIAN CLAIMING #####
		name = annex.ita
		trigger = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALG
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ITA = { add_state_claim = PREV }
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_ALG_nittified
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = { tag = ITA has_completed_focus = ITA_fifteenth_point }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = ALG_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Liberation
	id = annex.130
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.130" }
	title = annexation_LBA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_LBA_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = LBA }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 661 #Tripolitania
						state = 448 #Tripoli
						state = 449 #El Agheila
						state = 662 #Sirte
						state = 450 #Benghasi
						state = 663 #Cyrenaica
						state = 451 #Derna
						state = 273 #Libyan Desert
						state = 1199 #Fezzan
					}
				}
				add_core_of = LBA
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate Libya
		name = annex.130.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = FRA }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LBA
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			LBA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LBA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}
	option = { #Give to Italian Ally
		name = annex.130.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
					FIU = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
				}				
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			OR = {
				ITA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
				FIU = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LBA
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FIU = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LBA
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				FIU = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}

		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = FRA }
		}
		set_country_flag = LBA_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

	title = annexation_VOL_CONQ

					OR = {
						state = 681 #west cape

				add_core_of = VOL

country_event = { # Liberation
	id = annex.142
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.142" }
	title = annexation_TUN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_TUN_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = TUN }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 458 #Tunisia
						state = 665 #Gabes
					}
				}
				add_core_of = TUN
			}
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.142.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TUN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			TUN = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TUN }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			TUN = {
				set_politics = { 
					ruling_party = popular_socialism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = popular_socialism
					popularity = 0.30
				}
			}
			country_event = germany.42
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to Italian Ally
		name = annex.142.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			OR = {
				ITA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
				FIU = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FIU = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				FIU = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to French Ally
		name = annex.142.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			FRA = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TUN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			FRA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = TUN_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}
